# CQL Queries
create index on clicksImpressions(adId);
select numclicks from clicksImpressions where ownerId = 1 and adId = 3;
select numclicks from clicksImpressions where ownerId = 2;

===================== Cassandra: Python Code
#!/usr/bin/env python

# Copyright 2013-2014 DataStax, Inc.

import logging

log = logging.getLogger()
#log.setLevel('DEBUG')
log.setLevel('WARN')
handler = logging.StreamHandler()
handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s"))
log.addHandler(handler)

from cassandra import ConsistencyLevel
from cassandra.cluster import Cluster
from cassandra.query import SimpleStatement

KEYSPACE = "lab7python"


def main():
    cluster = Cluster(['127.0.0.1'])
    session = cluster.connect()

    log.info("creating keyspace...")

    session.execute("DROP KEYSPACE IF EXISTS " + KEYSPACE)
    
    session.execute("""
        CREATE KEYSPACE IF NOT EXISTS %s
        WITH replication = { 'class': 'SimpleStrategy', 'replication_factor': '2' }
        """ % KEYSPACE)

    log.info("setting keyspace...")

    session.set_keyspace(KEYSPACE)

    log.info("creating table...")
    session.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE clicksImpressions (
    OwnerId int,
    AdId int,
    numClicks int,
    numImpressions int,
    primary key (OwnerId, AdId)
    );
        """)

    vals =    [(1,1,1,10),
                (1,2,0,5),
                (1,3,1,20),
                (1,4,0,15),
                (2,1,0,10),
                (2,2,0,55),
                (2,3,0,13),
                (2,4,0,21),
                (3,1,1,32),
                (3,2,0,23),
                (3,3,2,44),
                (3,4,1,36)]

    query = SimpleStatement("""
        INSERT INTO clicksImpressions (OwnerId, AdId, numClicks, numImpressions)
        VALUES (%(key)s, %(a)s, %(b)s, %(c)s)
        """, consistency_level=ConsistencyLevel.ONE)

    prepared = session.prepare("""
        INSERT INTO clicksImpressions (OwnerId, AdId, numClicks, numImpressions)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
        """)



    for i in range(len(vals)):
        log.info("inserting row %d" % i)        
        session.execute(query, dict(key=vals[i][0], a=vals[i][1], b=vals[i][2], c=vals[i][3]) )
        #session.execute(query, dict(key="key%d", a='a', b='b', c ='c'))
        #session.execute(prepared, ("%s" % i, 'b', 'b'))

    future = session.execute_async("SELECT * FROM clicksImpressions")
    #print future
    log.info("key\tcol1\tcol2\tcol3")
    log.info("---\t----\t----\t")

    try:
        rows = future.result()
    except Exception:
        log.exeception()

    list = [];
    group_list = [0, 0, 0];
    # compute the numClicks / numImpressions
    print 'ownerId', '\t', 'adId', '\t', 'ctr'
    i = 0;
    for row in rows:
        list.append(float(row[2]) / float(row[3]));
        print row[0], '\t','\t', row[1], '\t', list[i];
        i = i + 1
        #log.info('\t'.join(row))

    # Compute the ctr for each owner
    i = 0;
    #print 'ctr for all owners'
    print 'ownerId', '\t', 'ctr'
    for row in rows:
        if (1 == row[0]):
            group_list[0] = group_list[0] + list[i];
        if (2 == row[0]):
            group_list[1] = group_list[1] + list[i];
        if (3 == row[0]):
            group_list[2] = group_list[2] + list[i];
        i = i + 1
    for i in range(len(group_list)):
        print (i + 1), '\t', '\t', group_list[i]


    future = session.execute_async("SELECT * FROM clicksImpressions")
    try:
        rows = future.result()
    except Exception:
        log.exeception()

    result = 0.00;
    for row in rows:
        #print row
        if ( (1 == row[0]) and (3 == row[1])):
            result += float(row[2]) / float(row[3]);

    print 'ownerId', 'adId', '\t', 'ctr'
    print '1', '\t', '3', '\t', result
    #print 'The Ctr for OwnerID 1, AdId 3', result


    # The Ctr for OwnerID = 2 is:
    print 'ownerId', '\t', 'ctr'
    print '2', '\t','\t', group_list[1]
    
    session.execute("DROP KEYSPACE " + KEYSPACE)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# Return cities that have population less than 5 million grouped by state
db.zipcodes.aggregate( {$group:  {_id: {state: "$state", city: "$city"}, pop: {$sum: "$pop"} } }, {$match: {pop : {$lt : 5000000}} }, {$group: {_id: "$_id.state", cities: {$push: "$_id.city"} } } )

#Return the cities with minimum population by state
